   "source": [
    "# Load the dataset\n",
    "df = pd.read_csv('Gold Price History.csv')\n",
    "\n",
    "# Basic data exploration\n",
    "print(\"First few rows of the dataset:\")\n",
    "print(df.head())\n",
    "\n",
    "print(\"\\nDataset shape:\", df.shape)\n",
    "print(\"\\nDataset info:\")\n",
    "print(df.info())\n",
    "print(\"\\nDataset description:\")\n",
    "print(df.describe())\n",
    "\n",
    "# Feature selection: Drop 'Volume' column and rename 'Close/Last' to 'Price'\n",
    "df.drop(['Volume'], axis=1, inplace=True)\n",
    "df.rename(columns={'Close/Last': 'Price'}, inplace=True)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Convert date column and sort\n",
    "df['Date'] = pd.to_datetime(df['Date'])\n",
    "df.sort_values(by='Date', ascending=True, inplace=True)\n",
    "df.reset_index(drop=True, inplace=True)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Remove redundant symbols and convert to float\n",
    "NumCols = df.columns.drop(['Date'])\n",
    "df[NumCols] = df[NumCols].replace({',': ''}, regex=True)\n",
    "df[NumCols] = df[NumCols].astype('float64')\n",
    "\n",
    "# Check for duplicates and missing values\n",
    "print(\"\\nNumber of duplicate rows:\", df.duplicated().sum())\n",
    "print(\"\\nNumber of missing values:\", df.isnull().sum().sum())\n",
    "\n",
    "# Data scaling\n",
    "scaler = MinMaxScaler()\n",
    "scaler.fit(df.Price.values.reshape(-1, 1))"
   ]

    "## 4. Data Splitting and Preparation"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 4,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [
    {
     "name": "stdout",
     "output_type": "stream",
     "text": [
      "Training data size: 2387\n",
      "Test data size: 143\n",
      "X_train Shape: (2327, 60, 1)\n",
      "y_train Shape: (2327,)\n",
      "X_test Shape: (143, 60, 1)\n",
      "y_test Shape: (143,)\n"
     ]
    }
   ],
   "source": [
    "\n",
    "\n",
    "# Filter data for training and testing\n",
    "train_data = df[df.Date.dt.year < 2024]\n",
    "test_data = df[df.Date.dt.year == 2024]\n",
    "\n",
    "# Print the sizes of the splits\n",
    "print(f\"Training data size: {train_data.shape[0]}\")\n",
    "print(f\"Test data size: {test_data.shape[0]}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# Data scaling\n",
    "scaler = MinMaxScaler()\n",
    "scaler.fit(df.Price.values.reshape(-1, 1))\n",
    "\n",
    "# Define window size\n",
    "window_size = 60\n",
    "\n",
    "def create_dataset(data, window_size):\n",
    "    X, y = [], []\n",
    "    for i in range(window_size, len(data)):\n",
    "        X.append(data[i-window_size:i, 0])\n",
    "        y.append(data[i, 0])\n",
    "    return np.array(X), np.array(y)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Create training set\n",
    "train_data = df.Price[:-test_size]\n",
    "train_data = scaler.transform(train_data.values.reshape(-1, 1))\n",
    "X_train, y_train = create_dataset(train_data, window_size)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Create test set\n",
    "test_data = df.Price[-test_size-window_size:]\n",
    "test_data = scaler.transform(test_data.values.reshape(-1, 1))\n",
    "X_test, y_test = create_dataset(test_data, window_size)\n",
    "\n",
    "# Reshape data to fit LSTM input requirements\n",
    "X_train = np.reshape(X_train, (X_train.shape[0], X_train.shape[1], 1))\n",
    "X_test = np.reshape(X_test, (X_test.shape[0], X_test.shape[1], 1))\n",
    "\n",
    "print('X_train Shape:', X_train.shape)\n",
    "print('y_train Shape:', y_train.shape)\n",
    "print('X_test Shape:', X_test.shape)\n",
    "print('y_test Shape:', y_test.shape)"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},
   "source": [
    "## 5.Model Definition"
   ]
  },
  {
   "cell_type": "code",
   "execution_count": 5,
   "metadata": {},
   "outputs": [],
   "source": [
    "\n",
    "# Define the model\n",
    "def define_model(window_size):\n",
    "    input1 = Input(shape=(window_size, 1))\n",
    "    x = LSTM(units=64, return_sequences=True)(input1)\n",
    "    x = Dropout(0.2)(x)\n",
    "    x = LSTM(units=64, return_sequences=True)(x)\n",
    "    x = Dropout(0.2)(x)\n",
    "    x = LSTM(units=64)(x)\n",
    "    x = Dropout(0.2)(x)\n",
    "    x = Dense(32, activation='relu')(x)\n",
    "    dnn_output = Dense(1)(x)\n",
    "\n",
    "    model = Model(inputs=input1, outputs=[dnn_output])\n",
    "    model.compile(loss='mean_squared_error', optimizer='Nadam')\n",
    "    model.summary()\n",
    "    \n",
    "    return model\n",
    "\n",
    "\n"
   ]
  },

   "cell_type": "markdown",
   "metadata": {},

    "# Plot the results\n",
    "plt.figure(figsize=(15, 6), dpi=150)\n",
    "plt.rc('axes', edgecolor='black', facecolor='white')\n",
    "plt.rc('figure', facecolor='white')\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.plot(df['Date'].iloc[:-test_size], scaler.inverse_transform(train_data), color='black', lw=2, label='Training Data')\n",
    "plt.plot(df['Date'].iloc[-test_size:], y_test_true, color='blue', lw=2, label='Actual Test Data')\n",
    "plt.plot(df['Date'].iloc[-test_size:], y_test_pred, color='red', lw=2, label='Predicted Test Data')\n",
    "\n",
    "plt.title('Model Performance on Gold Price Prediction', fontsize=15)\n",
    "plt.xlabel('Date', fontsize=12)\n",
    "plt.ylabel('Price', fontsize=12)\n",
    "plt.legend(loc='upper left', prop={'size': 15})\n",
    "plt.grid(color='gray')\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Visualize the training process\n",
    "plt.figure(figsize=(12, 6))\n",
    "plt.plot(history.history['loss'], label='Training Loss')\n",
    "plt.plot(history.history['val_loss'], label='Validation Loss')\n",
    "plt.title('Model Loss During Training')\n",
    "plt.xlabel('Epoch')\n",
    "plt.ylabel('Loss')\n",
    "plt.legend()\n",
    "plt.grid(True)\n",
    "plt.show()\n",
    "\n",
    "# Print final training and validation loss\n",
    "print(f\"Final training loss: {history.history['loss'][-1]:.4f}\")\n",
    "print(f\"Final validation loss: {history.history['val_loss'][-1]:.4f}\")\n",
    "\n",
    "# Calculate and plot the difference between training and validation loss\n",
    "plt.figure(figsize=(12, 6))\n",
    "loss_diff = np.array(history.history['loss']) - np.array(history.history['val_loss'])\n",
    "plt.plot(loss_diff, label='Training Loss - Validation Loss')\n",
    "plt.title('Difference Between Training and Validation Loss')\n",
    "plt.xlabel('Epoch')\n",
    "plt.ylabel('Loss Difference')\n",
    "plt.legend()\n",
    "plt.grid(True)\n",
    "plt.axhline(y=0, color='r', linestyle='--')\n",
    "plt.show()"
